**Notes:** 
DataHub includes pre-defined mapping templates that allow users to exchange data between MagicDraw with the SysML plugin, IBM Rational DOORS, Enovia TRM, and JAMA Connect. Other MagicDraw profiles are also supported, including CBM, UPDM, DoDAF, and any custom profile. 
 
[Click here to see the Cameo DataHub description.](http://www.nomagic.com/products/cameo-datahub.html)
